    { 1100525049;0;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table99;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Item No.,Variant Code,Vendor No.);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT AlternItemBl THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  TradeItem@1100525002 : Record 11012317;
                                  Item@1100525000 : Record 27;
                                BEGIN
                                  ItemBlocked := FALSE;
                                  ItemFound := TRUE;
                                  InvalidUnit := FALSE;
                                  ErrorCode := '';
                                  ItemDescription := '';

                                  IF "Vendor Item No." <>'' THEN BEGIN
                                    IF NOT TradeItem.GET("Vendor (Trade Item)", "Item Vendor"."Vendor Item No.") THEN
                                      ItemFound := FALSE
                                    ELSE
                                      IF TradeItem.Expired THEN
                                        ItemBlocked := TRUE;
                                  END;
                                  IF NOT CheckItemMeasure THEN
                                    InvalidUnit := TRUE;

                                  IF ItemFound = FALSE THEN
                                    ErrorCode := 'A'
                                  ELSE
                                    IF ItemBlocked = TRUE THEN
                                      ErrorCode := 'B'
                                    ELSE
                                      ErrorCode := 'C';

                                  IF ErrorCode = '' THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF Item.GET("Item No.") THEN
                                    ItemDescription := Item.Description;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Item No. }

  CODE
  {
    VAR
      SelectEstimate@1100525015 : Boolean;
      SelectRecipe@1100525014 : Boolean;
      SelectEstPartLines@1100525013 : Boolean;
      SelectBudgetLineProject@1100528900 : Boolean;
      SelectBudgetLineService@1100528901 : Boolean;

      ItemBlocked@1100525017 : Boolean;

      FooterInfo@1100525006 : Text[250];
      ErrorCode@1100525005 : Code[10];
      InvalidUnit@1100525004 : Boolean;
      AlternItemBl@1100525003 : Boolean;
      DescriptionTxt@1100525002 : Text[50];
      ItemCode@1100525001 : Code[20];
      ItemType@1100525000 : Code[10];
      ItemDescription@1100525010 : Text[100];

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100525000() : Text;
    BEGIN
      //IF Integer.GETFILTERS <> '' THEN
      //  EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', Integer.TABLECAPTION, Integer.GETFILTERS));
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckItem@1(ItemCode2@1210190000 : Code[20];BasicItemCode@1210190001 : Code[20];TradeItemCode@1210190002 : Code[20];ManufacturerCode@1210190004 : Code[20];VendorCode@1210190005 : Code[20];Desc@1210190006 : Text[100];UnitCode@1100485000 : Code[10]) : Boolean;
    VAR
      ItemUnitOfMeasure@1100485001 : Record 5404;
      TradeItem@1100525002 : Record 11012317;
      BasicItem@1100525001 : Record 11012316;
      Item@1100525000 : Record 27;
    BEGIN
      ItemFound := TRUE;
      ItemBlocked := FALSE;
      InvalidUnit := FALSE;
      ItemCode := '';
      MV := '';
      ErrorCode := '';

      IF TradeItemCode <> '' THEN BEGIN
        ItemCode := TradeItemCode;
        MV := VendorCode;
        ItemType := COPYSTR(TradeItem.TABLECAPTION, 1, 1);
        IF NOT TradeItem.GET(VendorCode, TradeItemCode) THEN
          ItemFound := FALSE
        ELSE
          ItemBlocked := TradeItem.Expired;
        IF ((UnitCode <> UPPERCASE(TradeItem."Application Unit")) AND
            (UnitCode <> UPPERCASE(TradeItem."Packaging Unit"))) OR
           (UnitCode = '') THEN
          InvalidUnit := TRUE;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        IF BasicItemCode <> '' THEN BEGIN
          ItemCode := BasicItemCode;
          MV := ManufacturerCode;
          ItemType := COPYSTR(BasicItem.TABLECAPTION, 1, 1);
          IF NOT BasicItem.GET(ManufacturerCode, BasicItemCode) THEN
            ItemFound := FALSE
          ELSE
            ItemBlocked := BasicItem.Expired;
          IF ((UnitCode <> UPPERCASE(BasicItem."Application Unit")) AND
              (UnitCode <> UPPERCASE(BasicItem."Packaging Unit"))) OR
             (UnitCode = '') THEN
            InvalidUnit := TRUE;
        END ELSE BEGIN
          IF ItemCode2 <> '' THEN BEGIN
            ItemCode := ItemCode2;
            MV := '';
            ItemType := COPYSTR(Item.TABLECAPTION, 1, 1);
            IF NOT Item.GET(ItemCode2) THEN
              ItemFound := FALSE
            ELSE
              ItemBlocked := Item.Blocked;
            IF NOT ItemUnitOfMeasure.GET(ItemCode2, UnitCode) THEN
              InvalidUnit := TRUE;
          END;
        END;
      END;

      //db.sn, 20-08-09: M14331
      IF (ItemFound = TRUE) AND (ItemBlocked = FALSE) AND (InvalidUnit = FALSE) THEN BEGIN
        IF (BasicItemCode + TradeItemCode <> '') AND (ItemCode2 <> '') THEN BEGIN
          ItemCode := ItemCode2;
          MV := '';
          ItemType := COPYSTR(Item.TABLECAPTION, 1, 1);
          IF NOT Item.GET(ItemCode2) THEN
            ItemFound := FALSE
          ELSE
            ItemBlocked := Item.Blocked;
          IF NOT ItemUnitOfMeasure.GET(ItemCode, UnitCode) THEN
            InvalidUnit := TRUE;
        END;
      END;
      //db.en, 20-08-09: M14331

      IF ItemFound = FALSE THEN
        ErrorCode := 'A'
      ELSE
        IF ItemBlocked = TRUE THEN
          ErrorCode := 'B'
        ELSE
          IF InvalidUnit = TRUE THEN
            ErrorCode := 'C';

      IF ErrorCode = '' THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      db, 16-01-14: do NOT fill ReqFilterFields for tables of module Service, due to problems with licence
    }
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
